27/**
28 * Serializes and Deserializes SObject records and related child and referenced records using the Apex JSON support
29 *
30 *   See https://github.com/afawcett/apex-sobjectdataloader for known issues, restrictions and TODO's
31 *
32 **/
33public with sharing class SobjectDataLoaderMVN 
34{
35    /**
36     * Configuration uses a Fluent method design (http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fluent_interface), 
37     **/
38    public class SerializeConfig
39    {
40        protected Set<Schema.SObjectField> followRelationships;
41        protected Set<Schema.SObjectField> followChildRelationships;
42        protected Set<Schema.SObjectField> omitFields;
43        
44        public SerializeConfig()
45        {    
46            followRelationships = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>();
47            followChildRelationships = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>();
48            omitFields = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>();             
49        }
50        
51        /**
52         * Provide a field that represents the lookup relationship the serializer should follow
53         **/
54        public SerializeConfig follow(Schema.SObjectField relationshipField)
55        {
56            followRelationships.add(relationshipField);
57            return this;
58        }
59        
60        /**
61         * Provide a field that represents a parent child relationship the serializer should follow
62         **/
63        public SerializeConfig followChild(Schema.SObjectField relationshipField)
64        {
65            followChildRelationships.add(relationshipField);
66            return this;
67        }
68        
69        /**
70         * Provide a field that the serializer should omit from the serialized output
71         **/
72        public SerializeConfig omit(Schema.SObjectField omitField)
73        {
74            omitFields.add(omitField);
75            if(followRelationships.contains(omitField))
76                followRelationships.remove(omitField);
77            if(followChildRelationships.contains(omitField))
78                followChildRelationships.remove(omitField);
79            return this;
80        }
81        
82        /** 
83         * Automatically configure (removes all previous configuration)
84         *  Skip known system lookup and child relationships but include the rest (direct children only) upto certain depth, 
85         *  Caller can always add or omit specific via follow or omit methods
86         **/
87        public SerializeConfig auto(Schema.SObjectType sObjectType)
88        {
89            followRelationships = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>();
90            followChildRelationships = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>();
91            omitFields = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>();
92            Set<Schema.SObjectType> searched = new Set<Schema.SObjectType>();
93            searchRelationships(sObjectType, 0, 0, true, searched);    
94            return this;    
95        }
96        
97        /**
98         * Seek out recursively relationships
99         **/
100        private void searchRelationships(Schema.SObjectType sObjectType, Integer lookupDepth, Integer childDepth, Boolean searchChildren, Set<Schema.SObjectType> searched)
101        {        
102            // Stop infinite recursion    
103            if(searched.contains(sObjectType) || lookupDepth > 2 || childDepth > 3) // TODO: Make max depth configurable
104                return;
105            searched.add(sObjectType);
106            Schema.DescribeSObjectResult sObjectDescribe = sObjectType.getDescribe();
107                        
108            // Following children? (only set for descendents of the top level object)
109            if(searchChildren)
110            {
111                List<Schema.ChildRelationship> childRelationships = sObjectDescribe.getChildRelationships();
112                for(Schema.ChildRelationship childRelationship : childRelationships)
113                {
114                    // Determine which child relationships to automatically follow
115                    String childRelationshipName = childRelationship.getRelationshipName();
116                    system.debug('=============== '+childRelationshipName);
117                    if(childRelationshipName==null || 
118                       childRelationshipWhitelist.contains(childRelationshipName)) // Skip relationships without names and those whitelisted
119                        continue;
120                    if(childRelationshipName.endsWith('Histories')) // Skip relationships ending in Histories (TODO: consider a RegEx approach?)
121                        continue;
122                    if(!childRelationship.isCascadeDelete()) // Skip relationships for none owned records (aka only follow master-detail relationships)
123                        continue;
124                    followChild(childRelationship.getField()).
125                        searchRelationships(childRelationship.getChildSObject(), lookupDepth, childDepth+1, true, searched);
126                }
127            }
128                            
129            // Follow lookup relationships to long as they have not previously been added as child references and are not whitelisted
130            Map<String, Schema.SObjectField> sObjectFields = sObjectDescribe.fields.getMap();
131            for(Schema.SObjectField sObjectField : sObjectFields.values())
132                if(sObjectField.getDescribe().getType() == Schema.DisplayType.Reference) 
133                    if(!followChildRelationships.contains(sObjectField) && !relationshipWhitelist.contains(sObjectField.getDescribe().getName()))
134                        follow(sObjectField).
135                            searchRelationships(sObjectField.getDescribe().getReferenceTo()[0], lookupDepth+1, childDepth, false, searched);
136        }
137
138        // Standard fields that are not included when using the auto config
139        private Set<String> relationshipWhitelist = 
140            new Set<String>
141                { 'OwnerId',
142                  'CreatedById',
143                  'LastModifiedById',
144                  'RecordTypeId'
145                };
146                
147        // Standard child relationships that are not included when using the auto config
148        private Set<String> childRelationshipWhitelist = 
149            new Set<String> 
150                { 'Shares', 
151                  'ProcessInstances', 
152                  'ProcessSteps', 
153                  'Tasks', 
154                  'ActivityHistories', 
155                  'Attachments', 
156                  'FeedSubscriptionsForEntity', 
157                  'Events', 
158                  'Notes', 
159                  'NotesAndAttachments', 
160                  'OpenActivities', 
161                  'Histories', 
162                  'Feeds',
163                  'PersonEmailStatuses',
164                  'OpenActivities',
165                  'PersonOpenActivities'};        
166    }
167    
168    
169    /**
170     * Serialize the given records using the default configuration (see SerializeConfig.auto)
171     **/
172    public static String serialize(Set<Id> ids)
173    {
174        // Serialize based on no prior knowledge of the objects
175        if(ids==null || ids.size()==0)
176            throw new SerializerException('List of Ids cannot be null or empty.');
177        return serialize(ids, new SerializeConfig().auto(new List<Id>(ids)[0].getSObjectType()));
178    }
179    
180    /**
181     * Serialize the given records using the given configuration
182     **/
183    public static String serialize(Set<Id> ids, SerializeConfig strategy)
184    {            
185        // Validate parameters
186        if(ids==null || ids.size()==0)
187            throw new SerializerException('List of Ids cannot be null or empty.');
188            
189        // Container to bundle record sets into 
190        RecordsBundle recordsToBundle = new RecordsBundle();
191        recordsToBundle.recordSetBundles = new List<RecordSetBundle>();        
192        recordsToBundle.recordSetBundlesByType = new Map<String, RecordSetBundle>();
193        
194        // Begin recursive serialize from given records through to related records
195        Schema.SObjectType sObjectType = new List<Id>(ids)[0].getSObjectType();
196        serialize(ids, sObjectType, null, strategy, 0, 0, recordsToBundle);
197                
198        // Serialise the records bundle container        
199        return JSON.serialize(recordsToBundle);                 
200    }
201
202    /**
203     * Deserialize the given JSON record set bundle
204     **/
205    public static Set<Id> deserialize(String recordsBundleAsJSON)
206    {
207        return deserialize(recordsBundleAsJSON, null);
208    }
209        
210    /**
211     * Deserialize the given JSON record set bundle utilising the given callback
212     **/
213    public static Set<Id> deserialize(String recordsBundleAsJSON, IDeserializeCallback callback)
214    {
215        // Desearialise the records bundle
216        RecordsBundle recordsBundle = (RecordsBundle) 
217            JSON.deserialize(recordsBundleAsJSON, SObjectDataLoaderMVN.RecordsBundle.class);
218        
219        // Map to track original ID's against the new SObject record instances being inserted
220        Map<Id, SObject> recordsByOriginalId = new Map<Id, SObject>();
221        
222        // Record set bundles are already ordered in dependency order due to serialisation approach
223        Map<String, Schema.SObjectType> sObjectsByType = Schema.getGlobalDescribe();
224        for(RecordSetBundle recordSetBundle : recordsBundle.recordSetBundles)
225        {
226            // Determine lookup / relationship fields to update prior to inserting these records
227            Schema.SObjectType sObjectType = sObjectsByType.get(recordSetBundle.ObjectType);
228            Map<String, Schema.SObjectField> sObjectFields = sObjectType.getDescribe().fields.getMap();
229            List<Schema.SObjectField> relationshipsFields = new List<Schema.SObjectField>();
230            for(Schema.SObjectField sObjectField : sObjectFields.values())
231                if(sObjectField.getDescribe().getType() == Schema.DisplayType.Reference) 
232                    relationshipsFields.add(sObjectField);
233                                    
234            // Prepare records for insert
235            List<SObject> recordsToInsert = new List<SObject>();
236            List<UnresolvedReferences> unresolvedReferencesByRecord = new List<UnresolvedReferences>(); 
237            for(SObject orignalRecord : recordSetBundle.Records)
238            {
239                // Clone the deserialised SObject to remove the original Id prior to inserting it
240                SObject newRecord = orignalRecord.clone();
241                recordsToInsert.add(newRecord);
242                // Map the new cloned record to its old Id (once inserted this can be used to obtain the new id)
243                recordsByOriginalId.put(orignalRecord.Id, newRecord);
244                // Update foreign key references / lookups / master-detail relationships
245                if(relationshipsFields.size()>0)
246                {
247                    Set<Schema.SObjectField> unresolvedFieldReferences = new Set<Schema.SObjectField>(); 
248                    for(Schema.SObjectField sObjectField : relationshipsFields)
249                    {                            
250                        // Obtained original related record Id and search map over new records by old Ids
251                        Id oldRelatedRecordId = (Id) orignalRecord.get(sObjectField);
252                        SObject newRelatedRecord = recordsByOriginalId.get(oldRelatedRecordId);
253                        if(newRelatedRecord!=null)
254                            newRecord.put(sObjectField, newRelatedRecord.Id);
255                        else
256                            unresolvedFieldReferences.add(sObjectField);
257                    }
258                    // Retain a list of records with unresolved references
259                    if(unresolvedFieldReferences.size()>0)
260                    {
261                        UnresolvedReferences unresolvedReferences = new UnresolvedReferences();
262                        unresolvedReferences.Record = newRecord;
263                        unresolvedReferences.References = unresolvedFieldReferences;
264                        unresolvedReferencesByRecord.add(unresolvedReferences);
265                    }    
266                }
267            }            
268            
269            // Let the caller attempt to resolve any references the above could not
270            if(callback!=null && unresolvedReferencesByRecord.size()>0)
271                callback.unresolvedReferences(sObjectType, unresolvedReferencesByRecord);
272            
273            // Insert cloned deserialised records
274            recordSetBundle.Records = recordsToInsert;
275            insert recordSetBundle.Records;
276        }
277        
278        // Return Id list from the first bundle set
279        return new Map<Id, SObject>(recordsBundle.recordSetBundles[0].Records).keySet();
280    }
281            
282    private static void serialize(Set<ID> ids, Schema.SObjectType sObjectType, Schema.SObjectField queryByIdField, SerializeConfig config, Integer lookupDepth, Integer childDepth, RecordsBundle recordsToBundle)
283    {        
284        // Config?
285        if(config==null)
286            throw new SerializerException('Must pass a valid SerializeConfig instance.');
287        // Stop infinite recursion
288        if(lookupDepth > 3 || childDepth > 3) // TODO: Make max depth configurable
289            return;
290            
291        // Describe object and determine fields to serialize
292        Schema.DescribeSObjectResult sObjectDesc = sObjectType.getDescribe();
293        Map<String, Schema.SObjectField> sObjectFields = sObjectDesc.fields.getMap();
294        List<Schema.SObjectField> sObjectFieldsToSerialize = listFieldsToSerialize(sObjectFields, config);
295                        
296        // Query records to serialize
297        String fieldList = null;
298        for(Schema.SObjectField sObjectField : sObjectFieldsToSerialize)
299            fieldList = fieldList == null ? sObjectField.getDescribe().getName() : fieldList + ',' + sObjectField.getDescribe().getName();
300        String query = String.format('select {0} from {1} where {2} in :ids order by {2}', 
301            new List<String> { fieldList, sObjectDesc.getName(), queryByIdField == null ? 'id' : queryByIdField.getDescribe().getName(), 'Name' });
302        System.debug('>>>>>>>>>>> '+query);
303        Map<Id, SObject> recordsToSerializeById = new Map<Id, SObject>(Database.query(query));
304        if(recordsToSerializeById.size()==0)
305            return;
306        
307        // Any lookup relationships to folow?
308        Set<Schema.SObjectField> sObjectFollowRelationships = config.followRelationships.clone();
309        sObjectFollowRelationships.retainAll(sObjectFields.values());
310        if(sObjectFollowRelationships.size()>0)
311        {                
312            // Build list of ID's for each related record
313            Map<Schema.DescribeFieldResult, Set<Id>> relationshipsByField = new Map<Schema.DescribeFieldResult, Set<Id>>(); 
314            for(Schema.SObjectField sObjectField : sObjectFollowRelationships)
315                relationShipsByField.put(sObjectField.getDescribe(), new Set<Id>() );            
316            for(SObject recordToSerialize : recordsToSerializeById.values())
317            {
318                for(Schema.DescribeFieldResult relationshipField : relationshipsByField.keySet())
319                {
320                    Id relatedId = (Id) recordToSerialize.get(relationshipField.getSObjectField());
321                    if(relatedId!=null)
322                        relationshipsByField.get(relationshipField).add(relatedId);
323                }
324            }
325            // Serialise related records
326            for(Schema.DescribeFieldResult relationshipField : relationshipsByField.keySet())
327            {
328                Set<Id> relatedRecordIds = relationshipsByField.get(relationshipField);
329                if(relatedRecordIds.size()>0)
330                    serialize(relatedRecordIds, relationshipField.getReferenceTo()[0], null, config, lookupDepth+1, childDepth, recordsToBundle);                    
331            }
332        }
333                    
334        // Add records to applicable record set bundle
335        RecordSetBundle recordSetBundle = recordsToBundle.recordSetBundlesByType.get(sObjectDesc.getName());
336        if(recordSetBundle!=null)
337        {
338            recordSetBundle.Records.addAll(recordsToSerializeById.values());
339        }
340        else if(recordSetBundle==null)
341        {
342            recordSetBundle = new RecordSetBundle();
343            recordSetBundle.ObjectType = sObjectDesc.getName();
344            recordSetBundle.Records = recordsToSerializeById.values();
345            recordsToBundle.recordSetBundles.add(recordSetBundle);
346            recordsToBundle.recordSetBundlesByType.put(recordSetBundle.ObjectType, recordSetBundle);
347        }
348                
349        // Any child relationships to follow?
350        List<Schema.ChildRelationship> childRelationships = sObjectDesc.getChildRelationships();
351        for(Schema.ChildRelationship childRelationship : childRelationships)
352        { 
353            // Is this a child relationship we have been asked to follow?
354            Schema.SObjectType childSObjectType = childRelationship.getChildSObject();
355            if(config.followChildRelationships.contains(childRelationship.getField()))
356                serialize(recordsToSerializeById.keySet(), childSObjectType, childRelationship.getField(), config, lookupDepth, childDepth+1, recordsToBundle);
357        }
358    }
359    
360    private static List<Schema.SObjectField> listFieldsToSerialize(Map<String, Schema.SObjectField> sObjectFields, SerializeConfig config)
361    {
362        // Filter fields to serialise
363        List<Schema.SObjectField> serializeFields = new List<Schema.SObjectField>(); 
364        List<String> fieldNames = new List<String>(sObjectFields.keySet());
365        fieldNames.sort();
366        for(String fieldName : fieldNames)
367        {
368            // Skip fields indicated in config
369            Schema.SObjectField sObjectField = sObjectFields.get(fieldName);
370            if(config.omitFields!=null && config.omitFields.contains(sObjectField))
371                continue;
372            // Skip read only fields, such as auto numbers and formula fields
373            Schema.DescribeFieldResult sObjectFieldDescribe = sObjectField.getDescribe();
374            if(sObjectFieldDescribe.isAutoNumber() ||
375               sObjectFieldDescribe.isCalculated())
376               continue;    
377            // Skip lookup fields not in either of the follow lists
378            if(sObjectFieldDescribe.getType() == Schema.DisplayType.Reference)
379                if(!(config.followRelationships.contains(sObjectField) ||
380                     config.followChildRelationships.contains(sObjectField)))
381                   continue;
382            // Serialize this field..                        
383            serializeFields.add(sObjectField);
384        }            
385        return serializeFields;    
386    }
387    
388    /** 
389     * General exception class
390     **/
391    public class SerializerException extends Exception
392    {
393        
394    }
395    
396    /**
397     * Callback used during deserialization
398     **/
399    public interface IDeserializeCallback
400    {
401        /**
402         * Used during deserialization to allow caller to attempt to resolve references not resolved but required to insert records
403         **/
404        void unresolvedReferences(Schema.SObjectType sObjectType, List<UnresolvedReferences> unresolvedReferences);
405    }
406    
407    /**
408     * Used during deserialization to allow caller to attempt to resolve references not resolved but required to insert records
409     **/
410    public class UnresolvedReferences
411    {
412        public SObject Record;
413        public Set<Schema.SObjectField> References;
414    }
415    
416    /**
417     * Internal Apex represnetation of the serialized output for all recordsets
418     **/
419    private class RecordsBundle
420    {
421        // Order of bundle sets is important
422        public List<RecordSetBundle> RecordSetBundles;            
423        // Used by serialiser to group records by type during recursion
424        public transient Map<String, RecordSetBundle> RecordSetBundlesByType;
425    }
426    
427    /**
428     * Internal Apex represnetation of the serialized output for a given recordset
429     **/
430    private class RecordSetBundle
431    {
432        // Groups records by type
433        public String ObjectType;
434        public List<SObject> Records;    
435    }
